---
title: "After Ubuntu Upgrade, Winodws 7 boot option is not visible in GRUB"
date: 2016-01-15
forum: Installation &amp; Upgrades
---

### Post by prasad14 on 2016-01-15
Hi 
I am new to Ubuntu World. 
After first Installation of Ubuntu 14.04, I used to see Windows 7 boot option on GRUB.
But today I upgraded ubuntu, and that option is not coming.

I tried editing grub.cfg file with the following entry:

### BEGIN /etc/grub.d/30_os-prober ###
menuentry "Windows 7 (loader) (on /dev/sda1)" {
    saved_entry=${chosen}
    save_env saved_entry
    insmod ntfs
    set root=(hd1,1)
    search --no-floppy --fs-uuid --set e0d4a286d4a25e92
    chainloader +1
}
### END /etc/grub.d/30_os-prober ###

After this I do see the Boot Option, but I do not know if this entry is correct because the uuid I could not find for my windows 7.
I feel that dev/sda1 is my Windows7.

Please help to get uuid for windows7. And help in correcting the entries above.

### Post by yancek on 2016-01-15
If windows is on sda1, the  set root=(hd1,1) is wrong.  Change it to set root=(hd0,1).  Grub counts drives from zero, partitions from one.

The uuid can be found with the command:  sudo blkid  Does that not work for you?  The letter in the UUID for a windows system always are uppercase, at least in my experience.  Not really sure that matters.

---

### Post by grahammechanical on 2016-01-15
This is what is written at the top of grub.cfg

> #
# DO NOT EDIT THIS FILE
#
# It is automatically generated by grub-mkconfig using templates
# from /etc/grub.d and settings from /etc/default/grub
#


If we run the command

```
sudo update-grub
```

it will run the grub-mkconfig command and generate entries in the 30_os-prober section of grub.cfg. There will be an output in the terminal window that will show all other operating systems detected. That output should show a record for Windows 7 boot loader.

How did you upgrade Ubuntu 14.04? Did you upgrade to newer version of Ubuntu?

Regards

---

Found memtest86+ image: /boot/memtest86+.elf
Found memtest86+ image: /boot/memtest86+.bin
done

No Windows Found.

I updated my entries as shown below: This is a kind of copying from the linux grub entry.

### BEGIN /etc/grub.d/30_os-prober ###
menuentry 'Windows 7 (loader) (on /dev/sda1)' {
    insmod part_msdos
    insmod ext2
    set root='hd0,msdos5'
    if [ x$feature_platform_search_hint = xy ]; then
      search --no-floppy --fs-uuid --set=root --hint-bios=hd0,msdos5 --hint-efi=hd0,msdos5 --hint-baremetal=ahci0,msdos5  40B9332A552F3F38
    else
      search --no-floppy --fs-uuid --set=root 40B9332A552F3F38
    fi
}
### END /etc/grub.d/30_os-prober ###

Sample grub entry for linux is as below:

menuentry 'Ubuntu' --class ubuntu --class gnu-linux --class gnu --class os $menuentry_id_option 'gnulinux-simple-35677980-c051-47fa-97d2-b75f198ca806' {
    recordfail
    load_video
    gfxmode $linux_gfx_mode
    insmod gzio
    insmod part_msdos
    insmod ext2
    set root='hd0,msdos5'
    if [ x$feature_platform_search_hint = xy ]; then
      search --no-floppy --fs-uuid --set=root --hint-bios=hd0,msdos5 --hint-efi=hd0,msdos5 --hint-baremetal=ahci0,msdos5  35677980-c051-47fa-97d2-b75f198ca806
    else
      search --no-floppy --fs-uuid --set=root 35677980-c051-47fa-97d2-b75f198ca806
    fi
    linux    /boot/vmlinuz-3.16.0-57-generic root=UUID=35677980-c051-47fa-97d2-b75f198ca806 ro  quiet splash $vt_handoff
    initrd    /boot/initrd.img-3.16.0-57-generic
}

After this change, I could see the option of Window 7 on Grub . But after clicking that it comes back on grub screen after 10 seconds.

Confused now.

### Post by oldfred on 2016-01-16
Did you download the 32 bit version of Ubuntu?
You really need the 64 bit version.

And is Windows installed in UEFI boot mode?
Ubuntu 32 bit will only install in BIOS boot mode and UEFI & BIOS are not compatible. You can only dual boot from UEFI menu as once you start booting in one mode you cannot switch. Or grub cannot change boot mode to boot any system not installed in same boot mode as grub boots.

---
